! ÅARAJEHTEDH even row A class I derived words -ehtedh, -estedh, -iste SOVVEDH ;
! GÅETEDH even row A class I derived words -gåete SOVVEDH ;
! TJEARODH even row C class II
! GUARKEDH even row B class III
! TJOEHPEDH even row D class IV
! GOEGKERDADTEDH even row D class IV derived words -alledh, -adte SOVVEDH ;
! SOVVEDH even row D class IV derived words -sovvedh, htalledh = passives
! AHTJE ! row D class IV derived words -ahtje
! VÅÅJNEDH even row E class V
! GÖÖLEDH even row F class VI
! GOLTELIDH odd !odd-syll with -adte- as Der2
! DÅAJVOEHTIDH odd !for stems ending -t-: dåajvoeht-, odd-syll with -alle- as Der2
! LGIDH odd ending -lgi SOVVEDH ;
! ------------------------------------
! Auxiliaries
! NEG
! LEA
! EDTJEDH



! First auxiliaries, then some irregular stray forms, 
! and then the full lexicon, ordered mainly by stem type
! (but the end of the doc has some lists). At some
! point we will alphabetise this file.


! Auxiliaries
! ===========

ij+V+Neg: NEG ;
lea+V: LEA ;
edtjedh+V:edtj EDTJEDH ;
olles:olle OLLE ;



! Irregular stray forms
! =====================

! Forms listed here are not generated by the paradigms
! in sma-lex.txt. Since they are idiosyncratic, we just list
! them here. If there arises a system on this list, it should
! be moved to sma-lex.txt.


! Lexical verbs
! =============
!mdidh-kladd

!don oainnát moai sáhtte dušše (buorre!) bidjat ná, ja de maŋŋil váldit olggos doublettaid? muhte mon gávnnan muhtin "vuoddo-vearbbaid nai, mat eai leat biddjon
!mun grep-en olggos gidh-vearbat dutnje? ja! mun maid gávnnan, mun sáhtán maid grepet olggos buot vuoddu-vearbbaid nai? in riekta ipmir manin, mu mielas lei buorre bargovuohki álggos
!ja, de moai ozzo geahccat fŋiereguhtem juohke ovtta/iesgudet(hver og et?) sáni: jua! ja de moai buoribut dihte. ok, moai jotke ná.
!didh
